197→\t\t\t\t\tgo notifier.Start()\n   198→\t\t\t\t\tm.thresholdNotifiers = append(m.thresholdNotifiers, notifier)\n   199→\t\t\t\t}\n   200→\t\t\t}\n   201→\t\t}\n   202→\t}\n   203→\t// start the eviction manager monitoring\n   204→\tgo func() {\n   205→\t\tfor {\n   206→\t\t\tevictedPods, err := m.synchronize(diskInfoProvider, podFunc)\n   207→\t\t\tif evictedPods != nil && err == nil {\n   208→\t\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: pods evicted, waiting for pod to be cleaned up\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(evictedPods))\n   209→\t\t\t\tm.waitForPodsCleanup(podCleanedUpFunc, evictedPods)\n   210→\t\t\t} else {\n   211→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   212→\t\t\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Eviction manager: failed to synchronize\")\n   213→\t\t\t\t}\n   214→\t\t\t\ttime.Sleep(monitoringInterval)\n   215→\t\t\t}\n   216→\t\t}\n   217→\t}()\n   218→}\n   219→\n   220→// IsUnderMemoryPressure returns true if the node is under memory pressure.\n   221→func (m *managerImpl) IsUnderMemoryPressure() bool {\n   222→\tm.RLock()\n   223→\tdefer m.RUnlock()\n   224→\treturn hasNodeCondition(m.nodeConditions, v1.NodeMemoryPressure)\n   225→}\n   226→\n   227→// IsUnderDiskPressure returns true if the node is under disk pressure.\n   228→func (m *managerImpl) IsUnderDiskPressure() bool {\n   229→\tm.RLock()\n   230→\tdefer m.RUnlock()\n   231→\treturn hasNodeCondition(m.nodeConditions, v1.NodeDiskPressure)\n   232→}\n   233→\n   234→// IsUnderPIDPressure returns true if the node is under PID pressure.\n   235→func (m *managerImpl) IsUnderPIDPressure() bool {\n   236→\tm.RLock()\n   237→\tdefer m.RUnlock()\n   238→\treturn hasNodeCondition(m.nodeConditions, v1.NodePIDPressure)\n   239→}\n   240→\n   241→// synchronize is the main control loop that enforces eviction thresholds.\n   242→// Returns the pod that was killed, or nil if no pod was killed.\n   243→func (m *managerImpl) synchronize(diskInfoProvider DiskInfoProvider, podFunc ActivePodsFunc) ([]*v1.Pod, error) {\n   244→\tctx := context.Background()\n   245→\t// if we have nothing to do, just return\n   246→\tthresholds := m.config.Thresholds\n   247→\tif len(thresholds) == 0 && !m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n   248→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   249→\t}\n   250→\n   251→\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: synchronize housekeeping\")\n   252→\t// build the ranking functions (if not yet known)\n   253→\t// TODO: have a function in cadvisor that lets us know if global housekeeping has completed\n   254→\tif m.dedicatedImageFs == nil {\n   255→\t\thasImageFs, imageFsErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedImageFs(ctx)\n   256→\t\tif imageFsErr != nil {\n   257→\t\t\t// TODO: This should be refactored to log an error and retry the HasDedicatedImageFs\n   258→\t\t\t// If we have a transient error this will never be retried and we will not set eviction signals\n   259→\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(imageFsErr, \"Eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs\")\n   260→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs: %w\", imageFsErr)\n   261→\t\t}\n   262→\t\tm.dedicatedImageFs = &hasImageFs\n   263→\t\tsplitContainerImageFs, splitErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedContainerFs(ctx)\n   264→\t\tif splitErr != nil {\n   265→\t\t\t// A common error case is when there is no split filesystem\n   266→\t\t\t// there is an error finding the split filesystem label and we want to ignore these errors\n   267→\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(splitErr, \"eviction manager: failed to check if we have separate container filesystem. Ignoring.\")\n   268→\t\t}\n   269→\n   270→\t\t// If we are a split filesystem but the feature is turned off\n   271→\t\t// we should return an error.\n   272→\t\t// This is a bad state.\n   273→\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.KubeletSeparateDiskGC) && splitContainerImageFs {\n   274→\t\t\tsplitDiskError := fmt.Errorf(\"KubeletSeparateDiskGC is turned off but we still have a split filesystem\")\n   275→\t\t\treturn nil, splitDiskError\n   276→\t\t}\n   277→\t\tthresholds, err := UpdateContainerFsThresholds(m.config.Thresholds, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n   278→\t\tm.config.Thresholds = thresholds\n   279→\t\tif err != nil {\n   280→\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"eviction manager: found conflicting containerfs eviction. Ignoring.\")\n   281→\t\t}\n   282→\t\tm.splitContainerImageFs = &splitContainerImageFs\n   283→\t\tm.signalToRankFunc = buildSignalToRankFunc(hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n   284→\t\tm.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs = buildSignalToNodeReclaimFuncs(m.imageGC, m.containerGC, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n   285→\t}\n   286→\n   287→\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"FileSystem detection\", \"DedicatedImageFs\", m.dedicatedImageFs, \"SplitImageFs\", m.splitContainerImageFs)\n   288→\tactivePods := podFunc()\n   289→\tupdateStats := true\n   290→\tsummary, err := m.summaryProvider.Get(ctx, updateStats)\n   291→\tif err != nil {\n   292→\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Eviction manager: failed to get summary stats\")\n   293→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   294→\t}\n   295→\n   296→\tif m.clock.Since(m.thresholdsLastUpdated) > notifierRefreshInterval {\n   297→\t\tm.thresholdsLastUpdated = m.clock.Now()\n   298→\t\tfor _, notifier := range m.thresholdNotifiers {\n   299→\t\t\tif err := notifier.UpdateThreshold(summary); err != nil {\n   300→\t\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: failed to update notifier\", \"notifier\", notifier.Description(), \"err\", err)\n   301→\t\t\t}\n   302→\t\t}\n   303→\t}\n   304→\n   305→\t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n   306→\tobservations, statsFunc := makeSignalObservations(summary)\n   307→\tdebugLogObservations(\"observations\", observations)\n   308→\n   309→\t// determine the set of thresholds met independent of grace period\n   310→\tthresholds = thresholdsMet(thresholds, observations, false)\n   311→\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - ignoring grace period\", thresholds, observations)\n   312→\n   313→\t// determine the set of thresholds previously met that have not yet satisfied the associated min-reclaim\n   314→\tif len(m.thresholdsMet) > 0 {\n   315→\t\tthresholdsNotYetResolved := thresholdsMet(m.thresholdsMet, observations, true)\n   316→\t\tthresholds = mergeThresholds(thresholds, thresholdsNotYetResolved)\n   317→\t}\n   318→\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - reclaim not satisfied\", thresholds, observations)\n   319→\n   320→\t// track when a threshold was first observed\n   321→\tnow := m.clock.Now()\n   322→\tthresholdsFirstObservedAt := thresholdsFirstObservedAt(thresholds, m.thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\n   323→\n   324→\t// the set of node conditions that are triggered by currently observed thresholds\n   325→\tnodeConditions := nodeConditions(thresholds)\n   326→\tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n   327→\t\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - observed\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n   328→\t}\n   329→\n   330→\t// track when a node condition was last observed\n   331→\tnodeConditionsLastObservedAt := nodeConditionsLastObservedAt(nodeConditions, m.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, now)\n   332→\n   333→\t// node conditions report true if it has been observed within the transition period window\n   334→\tnodeConditions = nodeConditionsObservedSince(nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, m.config.PressureTransitionPeriod, now)\n   335→\tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n   336→\t\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - transition period not met\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n   337→\t}\n   338→\n   339→\t// determine the set of thresholds we need to drive eviction behavior (i.e. all grace periods are met)\n   340→\tthresholds = thresholdsMetGracePeriod(thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\n   341→\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - grace periods satisfied\", thresholds, observations)\n   342→\n   343→\t// update internal state\n   344→\tm.Lock()\n   345→\tm.nodeConditions = nodeConditions\n   346→\tm.thresholdsFirstObservedAt = thresholdsFirstObservedAt\n   347→\tm.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt = nodeConditionsLastObservedAt\n   348→\tm.thresholdsMet = thresholds\n   349→\n   350→\t// determine the set of thresholds whose stats have been updated since the last sync\n   351→\tthresholds = thresholdsUpdatedStats(thresholds, observations, m.lastObservations)\n   352→\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - updated stats\", thresholds, observations)\n   353→\n   354→\tm.lastObservations = observations\n   355→\tm.Unlock()\n   356→\n   357→\t// evict pods if there is a resource usage violation from local volume temporary storage\n   358→\t// If eviction happens in localStorageEviction function, skip the rest of eviction action\n   359→\tif m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n   360→\t\tif evictedPods := m.localStorageEviction(activePods, statsFunc); len(evictedPods) > 0 {\n   361→\t\t\treturn evictedPods, nil\n   362→\t\t}\n   363→\t}\n   364→\n   365→\tif len(thresholds) == 0 {\n   366→\t\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: no resources are starved\")\n   367→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   368→\t}\n   369→\n   370→\t// rank the thresholds by eviction priority\n   371→\tsort.Sort(byEvictionPriority(thresholds))\n   372→\tthresholdToReclaim, resourceToReclaim, foundAny := getReclaimableThreshold(thresholds)\n   373→\tif !foundAny {\n   374→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   375→\t}\n   376→\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: attempting to reclaim\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n   377→\n   378→\t// record an event about the resources we are now attempting to reclaim via eviction\n   379→\tm.recorder.Eventf(m.nodeRef, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"EvictionThresholdMet\", \"Attempting to reclaim %s\", resourceToReclaim)\n   380→\n   381→\t// check if there are node-level resources we can reclaim to reduce pressure before evicting end-user pods.\n   382→\tif m.reclaimNodeLevelResources(ctx, thresholdToReclaim.Signal, resourceToReclaim) {\n   383→\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: able to reduce resource pressure without evicting pods.\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n   384→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   385→\t}\n   386→\n   387→\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: must evict pod(s) to reclaim\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n   388→\n   389→\t// rank the pods for eviction\n   390→\trank, ok := m.signalToRankFunc[thresholdToReclaim.Signal]\n   391→\tif !ok {\n   392→\t\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \"Eviction manager: no ranking function for signal\", \"threshold\", thresholdToReclaim.Signal)\n   393→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   394→\t}\n   395→\n   396→\t// the only candidates viable for eviction are those pods that had anything running.\n   397→\tif len(activePods) == 0 {\n   398→\t\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \"Eviction manager: eviction thresholds have been met, but no pods are active to evict\")\n   399→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   400→\t}\n   401→\n   402→\t// rank the running pods for eviction for the specified resource\n   403→\trank(activePods, statsFunc)\n   404→\n   405→\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: pods ranked for eviction\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(activePods))\n   406→\n   407→\t//record age of metrics for met thresholds that we are using for evictions.\n   408→\tfor _, t := range thresholds {\n   409→\t\ttimeObserved := observations[t.Signal].time\n   410→\t\tif !timeObserved.IsZero() {\n   411→\t\t\tmetrics.EvictionStatsAge.WithLabelValues(string(t.Signal)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(timeObserved.Time))\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t}\n   414→\n   415→\t// we kill at most a single pod during each eviction interval\n   416→\tfor i := range activePods {\n   417→\t\tpod := activePods[i]\n   418→\t\tgracePeriodOverride := int64(immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds)\n   419→\t\tif !isHardEvictionThreshold(thresholdToReclaim) {\n   420→\t\t\tgracePeriodOverride = m.config.MaxPodGracePeriodSeconds\n   421→\t\t\tif pod.Spec.TerminationGracePeriodSeconds != nil && !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.AllowOverwriteTerminationGracePeriodSeconds) {\n   422→\t\t\t\tgracePeriodOverride = min(m.config.MaxPodGracePeriodSeconds, *pod.Spec.TerminationGracePeriodSeconds)\n   423→\t\t\t}\n   424→\t\t}\n   425→\n   426→\t\tmessage, annotations := evictionMessage(resourceToReclaim, pod, statsFunc, thresholds, observations)\n   427→\t\tcondition := &v1.PodCondition{\n   428→\t\t\tType:    v1.DisruptionTarget,\n   429→\t\t\tStatus:  v1.ConditionTrue,\n   430→\t\t\tReason:  v1.PodReasonTerminationByKubelet,\n   431→\t\t\tMessage: message,\n   432→\t\t}\n   433→\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, gracePeriodOverride, message, annotations, condition) {\n   434→\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(string(thresholdToReclaim.Signal)).Inc()\n   435→\t\t\treturn []*v1.Pod{pod}, nil\n   436→\t\t}\n   437→\t}\n   438→\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: unable to evict any pods from the node\")\n   439→\treturn nil, nil\n   440→}\n   441→\n   442→func (m *managerImpl) waitForPodsCleanup(podCleanedUpFunc PodCleanedUpFunc, pods []*v1.Pod) {\n   443→\ttimeout := m.clock.NewTimer(podCleanupTimeout)\n   444→\tdefer timeout.Stop()\n   445→\tticker := m.clock.NewTicker(podCleanupPollFreq)\n   446→\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n   447→\tfor {\n   448→\t\tselect {\n   449→\t\tcase <-timeout.C():\n   450→\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: timed out waiting for pods to be cleaned up\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods))\n   451→\t\t\treturn\n   452→\t\tcase <-ticker.C():\n   453→\t\t\tfor i, pod := range pods {\n   454→\t\t\t\tif !podCleanedUpFunc(pod) {\n   455→\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   456→\t\t\t\t}\n   457→\t\t\t\tif i == len(pods)-1 {\n   458→\t\t\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: pods successfully cleaned up\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods))\n   459→\t\t\t\t\treturn\n   460→\t\t\t\t}\n   461→\t\t\t}\n   462→\t\t}\n   463→\t}\n   464→}\n   465→\n   466→// reclaimNodeLevelResources attempts to reclaim node level resources.  returns true if thresholds were satisfied and no pod eviction is required.\n   467→func (m *managerImpl) reclaimNodeLevelResources(ctx context.Context, signalToReclaim evictionapi.Signal, resourceToReclaim v1.ResourceName) bool {\n   468→\tnodeReclaimFuncs := m.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs[signalToReclaim]\n   469→\tfor _, nodeReclaimFunc := range nodeReclaimFuncs {\n   470→\t\t// attempt to reclaim the pressured resource.\n   471→\t\tif err := nodeReclaimFunc(ctx); err != nil {\n   472→\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: unexpected error when attempting to reduce resource pressure\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim, \"err\", err)\n   473→\t\t}\n   474→\n   475→\t}\n   476→\tif len(nodeReclaimFuncs) > 0 {\n   477→\t\tsummary, err := m.summaryProvider.Get(ctx, true)\n   478→\t\tif err != nil {\n   479→\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Eviction manager: failed to get summary stats after resource reclaim\")\n   480→\t\t\treturn false\n   481→\t\t}\n   482→\n   483→\t\t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n   484→\t\tobservations, _ := makeSignalObservations(summary)\n   485→\t\tdebugLogObservations(\"observations after resource reclaim\", observations)\n   486→\n   487→\t\t// evaluate all thresholds independently of their grace period to see if with\n   488→\t\t// the new observations, we think we have met min reclaim goals\n   489→\t\tthresholds := thresholdsMet(m.config.Thresholds, observations, true)\n   490→\t\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds after resource reclaim - ignoring grace period\", thresholds, observations)\n   491→\n   492→\t\tif len(thresholds) == 0 {\n   493→\t\t\treturn true\n   494→\t\t}\n   495→\t}\n   496→\treturn false\n   497→}\n   498→\n   499→// localStorageEviction checks the EmptyDir volume usage for each pod and determine whether it exceeds the specified limit and needs\n   500→// to be evicted. It also checks every container in the pod, if the container overlay usage exceeds the limit, the pod will be evicted too.\n   501→func (m *managerImpl) localStorageEviction(pods []*v1.Pod, statsFunc statsFunc) []*v1.Pod {\n   502→\tevicted := []*v1.Pod{}\n   503→\tfor _, pod := range pods {\n   504→\t\tpodStats, ok := statsFunc(pod)\n   505→\t\tif !ok {\n   506→\t\t\tcontinue\n   507→\t\t}\n   508→\n   509→\t\tif m.emptyDirLimitEviction(podStats, pod) {\n   510→\t\t\tevicted = append(evicted, pod)\n   511→\t\t\tcontinue\n   512→\t\t}\n   513→\n   514→\t\tif m.podEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats, pod) {\n   515→\t\t\tevicted = append(evicted, pod)\n   516→\t\t\tcontinue\n   517→\t\t}\n   518→\n   519→\t\tif m.containerEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats, pod) {\n   520→\t\t\tevicted = append(evicted, pod)\n   521→\t\t}\n   522→\t}\n   523→\n   524→\treturn evicted\n   525→}\n   526→\n   527→func (m *managerImpl) emptyDirLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n   528→\tpodVolumeUsed := make(map[string]*resource.Quantity)\n   529→\tfor _, volume := range podStats.VolumeStats {\n   530→\t\tpodVolumeUsed[volume.Name] = resource.NewQuantity(int64(*volume.UsedBytes), resource.BinarySI)\n   531→\t}\n   532→\tfor i := range pod.Spec.Volumes {\n   533→\t\tsource := &pod.Spec.Volumes[i].VolumeSource\n   534→\t\tif source.EmptyDir != nil {\n   535→\t\t\tsize := source.EmptyDir.SizeLimit\n   536→\t\t\tused := podVolumeUsed[pod.Spec.Volumes[i].Name]\n   537→\t\t\tif used != nil && size != nil && size.Sign() == 1 && used.Cmp(*size) > 0 {\n   538→\t\t\t\t// the emptyDir usage exceeds the size limit, evict the pod\n   539→\t\t\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, fmt.Sprintf(emptyDirMessageFmt, pod.Spec.Volumes[i].Name, size.String()), nil, nil) {\n   540→\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEmptyDirFsLimit).Inc()\n   541→\t\t\t\t\treturn true\n   542→\t\t\t\t}\n   543→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   544→\t\t\t}\n   545→\t\t}\n   546→\t}\n   547→\n   548→\treturn false\n   549→}\n   550→\n   551→func (m *managerImpl) podEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n   552→\tpodLimits := resourcehelper.PodLimits(pod, resourcehelper.PodResourcesOptions{})\n   553→\t_, found := podLimits[v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage]\n   554→\tif !found {\n   555→\t\treturn false\n   556→\t}\n   557→\n   558→\t// pod stats api summarizes ephemeral storage usage (container, emptyDir, host[etc-hosts, logs])\n   559→\tpodEphemeralStorageTotalUsage := &resource.Quantity{}\n   560→\tif podStats.EphemeralStorage != nil && podStats.EphemeralStorage.UsedBytes != nil {\n   561→\t\tpodEphemeralStorageTotalUsage = resource.NewQuantity(int64(*podStats.EphemeralStorage.UsedBytes), resource.BinarySI)\n   562→\t}\n   563→\tpodEphemeralStorageLimit := podLimits[v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage]\n   564→\tif podEphemeralStorageTotalUsage.Cmp(podEphemeralStorageLimit) > 0 {\n   565→\t\t// the total usage of pod exceeds the total size limit of containers, evict the pod\n   566→\t\tmessage := fmt.Sprintf(podEphemeralStorageMessageFmt, podEphemeralStorageLimit.String())\n   567→\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, message, nil, nil) {\n   568→\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEphemeralPodFsLimit).Inc()\n   569→\t\t\treturn true\n   570→\t\t}\n   571→\t\treturn false\n   572→\t}\n   573→\treturn false\n   574→}\n   575→\n   576→func (m *managerImpl) containerEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n   577→\tthresholdsMap := make(map[string]*resource.Quantity)\n   578→\tfor _, container := range pod.Spec.Containers {\n   579→\t\tephemeralLimit := container.Resources.Limits.StorageEphemeral()\n   580→\t\tif ephemeralLimit != nil && ephemeralLimit.Value() != 0 {\n   581→\t\t\tthresholdsMap[container.Name] = ephemeralLimit\n   582→\t\t}\n   583→\t}\n   584→\n   585→\tfor _, containerStat := range podStats.Containers {\n   586→\t\tcontainerUsed := diskUsage(containerStat.Logs)\n   587→\t\tif !*m.dedicatedImageFs {\n   588→\t\t\tcontainerUsed.Add(*diskUsage(containerStat.Rootfs))\n   589→\t\t}\n   590→\n   591→\t\tif ephemeralStorageThreshold, ok := thresholdsMap[containerStat.Name]; ok {\n   592→\t\t\tif ephemeralStorageThreshold.Cmp(*containerUsed) < 0 {\n   593→\t\t\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, fmt.Sprintf(containerEphemeralStorageMessageFmt, containerStat.Name, ephemeralStorageThreshold.String()), nil, nil) {\n   594→\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEphemeralContainerFsLimit).Inc()\n   595→\t\t\t\t\treturn true\n   596→\t\t\t\t}\n   597→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   598→\t\t\t}\n   599→\t\t}\n   600→\t}\n   601→\treturn false\n   602→}\n   603→\n   604→func (m *managerImpl) evictPod(pod *v1.Pod, gracePeriodOverride int64, evictMsg string, annotations map[string]string, condition *v1.PodCondition) bool {\n   605→\t// If the pod is marked as critical and static, and support for critical pod annotations is enabled,\n   606→\t// do not evict such pods. Static pods are not re-admitted after evictions.\n   607→\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/40573 has more details.\n   608→\tif kubelettypes.IsCriticalPod(pod) {\n   609→\t\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \"Eviction manager: cannot evict a critical pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n   610→\t\treturn false\n   611→\t}\n   612→\t// record that we are evicting the pod\n   613→\tm.recorder.AnnotatedEventf(pod, annotations, v1.EventTypeWarning, Reason, evictMsg)\n   614→\t// this is a blocking call and should only return when the pod and its containers are killed.\n   615→\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Evicting pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podUID\", pod.UID, \"message\", evictMsg)\n   616→\terr := m.killPodFunc(pod, true, &gracePeriodOverride, func(status *v1.PodStatus) {\n   617→\t\tstatus.Phase = v1.PodFailed\n   618→\t\tstatus.Reason = Reason\n   619→\t\tstatus.Message = evictMsg\n   620→\t\tif condition != nil {\n   621→\t\t\tpodutil.UpdatePodCondition(status, condition)\n   622→\t\t}\n   623→\t})\n   624→\tif err != nil {\n   625→\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Eviction manager: pod failed to evict\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n   626→\t} else {\n   627→\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: pod is evicted successfully\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n   628→\t}\n   629→\treturn true\n   630→}\n   631→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. false,\n\t\tReason:  Reason,\n\t\tMessage: fmt.Sprintf(nodeConditionMessageFmt, m.nodeConditions),\n\t}\n}\n\n// Start starts the control loop to observe and response to low compute resources.\nfunc (m *managerImpl) Start(diskInfoProvider DiskInfoProvider, podFunc ActivePodsFunc, podCleanedUpFunc PodCleanedUpFunc, monitoringInterval time.Duration) {\n\tthresholdHandler := func(message string) {\n\t\tklog.InfoS(message)\n\t\tm.synchronize(diskInfoProvider, podFunc)\n\t}\n\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: starting control loop\")\n\tif m.config.KernelMemcgNotification || runtime.GOOS == pressure.\nfunc (m *managerImpl) IsUnderDiskPressure() bool {\n\tm.RLock()\n\tdefer m.RUnlock()\n\treturn hasNodeCondition(m.nodeConditions, v1.NodeDiskPressure)\n}\n\n// IsUnderPIDPressure returns synchronize is the main control loop that enforces eviction thresholds.\n// Returns the pod that was killed, or nil if no pod was killed.\nfunc (m *managerImpl) synchronize(diskInfoProvider DiskInfoProvider, podFunc ActivePodsFunc) ([]*v1.Pod, error) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\t// if we have nothing to do, just return\n\tthresholds := m.config.Thresholds\n\tif len(thresholds) == 0 && !m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: synchronize housekeeping\")\n\t// build the ranking functions (if not yet known)\n\t// TODO: have a function in cadvisor that lets us know if global housekeeping has completed\n\tif m.dedicatedImageFs == nil {\n\t\thasImageFs, imageFsErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedImageFs(ctx)\n\t\tif imageFsErr != nil {\n\t\t\t// TODO: This should be refactored to log an error and retry the HasDedicatedImageFs\n\t\t\t// If we have a transient error this will never be retried and we will not set eviction signals\n\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(imageFsErr, \"Eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs\")\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs: %w\", imageFsErr)\n\t\t}\n\t\tm.dedicatedImageFs = &hasImageFs\n\t\tsplitContainerImageFs, splitErr := diskInfoProvider.HasDedicatedContainerFs(ctx)\n\t\tif splitErr != nil {\n\t\t\t// A common error case if we have separate container filesystem. Ignoring.\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If we are a split filesystem but the feature is turned off\n\t\t// we should return an error.\n\t\t// This is a bad state.\n\t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.KubeletSeparateDiskGC) && splitContainerImageFs {\n\t\t\tsplitDiskError := fmt.Errorf(\"KubeletSeparateDiskGC is turned off but we still have a split filesystem\")\n\t\t\treturn nil, splitDiskError\n\t\t}\n\t\tthresholds, err := UpdateContainerFsThresholds(m.config.Thresholds, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n\t\tm.config.Thresholds = thresholds\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"eviction manager: found conflicting containerfs eviction. Ignoring.\")\n\t\t}\n\t\tm.splitContainerImageFs = &splitContainerImageFs\n\t\tm.signalToRankFunc = buildSignalToRankFunc(hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n\t\tm.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs = \"SplitImageFs\", m.splitContainerImageFs)\n\tactivePods := podFunc()\n\tupdateStats := true\n\tsummary, err := m.summaryProvider.Get(ctx, updateStats)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, m.clock.Now()\n\t\tfor _, notifier := range m.thresholdNotifiers {\n\t\t\tif err := notifier.UpdateThreshold(summary); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: failed to update notifier\", \"notifier\", notifier.Description(), \"err\", err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n\tobservations, statsFunc := makeSignalObservations(summary)\n\tdebugLogObservations(\"observations\", observations)\n\n\t// determine the set of thresholds met independent of grace period\n\tthresholds = thresholdsMet(thresholds, observations, false)\n\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - ignoring grace period\", thresholds, observations)\n\n\t// determine the set of thresholds previously met that have not yet satisfied the associated min-reclaim\n\tif len(m.thresholdsMet) > 0 {\n\t\tthresholdsNotYetResolved := thresholdsMet(m.thresholdsMet, observations, true)\n\t\tthresholds = mergeThresholds(thresholds, thresholdsNotYetResolved)\n\t}\n\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - reclaim not satisfied\", thresholds, observations)\n\n\t// track when a threshold was first observed\n\tnow := m.clock.Now()\n\tthresholdsFirstObservedAt := thresholdsFirstObservedAt(thresholds, m.thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\n\n\t// the set of node conditions that are triggered by currently observed thresholds\n\tnodeConditions := nodeConditions(thresholds)\n\tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n\t\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - observed\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n\t}\n\n\t// track when a node condition was last observed\n\tnodeConditionsLastObservedAt := nodeConditionsLastObservedAt(nodeConditions, m.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, now)\n\n\t// node conditions report true if it has been observed within the transition period window\n\tnodeConditions = nodeConditionsObservedSince(nodeConditionsLastObservedAt, m.config.PressureTransitionPeriod, now)\n\tif len(nodeConditions) > 0 {\n\t\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: node conditions - transition period not met\", \"nodeCondition\", nodeConditions)\n\t}\n\n\t// determine the set of thresholds we need to drive eviction behavior (i.e. all grace periods are met)\n\tthresholds = thresholdsMetGracePeriod(thresholdsFirstObservedAt, now)\n\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - grace periods satisfied\", thresholds, observations)\n\n\t// update internal state\n\tm.Lock()\n\tm.nodeConditions = nodeConditions\n\tm.thresholdsFirstObservedAt = thresholdsFirstObservedAt\n\tm.nodeConditionsLastObservedAt = nodeConditionsLastObservedAt\n\tm.thresholdsMet = thresholds\n\n\t// determine the set of thresholds whose stats have been updated since the last sync\n\tthresholds = thresholdsUpdatedStats(thresholds, observations, m.lastObservations)\n\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds - updated stats\", thresholds, observations)\n\n\tm.lastObservations = observations\n\tm.Unlock()\n\n\t// evict pods if there is a resource usage violation from local volume temporary storage\n\t// If eviction happens in localStorageEviction function, skip the rest of eviction action\n\tif m.localStorageCapacityIsolation {\n\t\tif evictedPods := m.localStorageEviction(activePods, statsFunc); len(evictedPods) > 0 {\n\t\t\treturn evictedPods, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif len(thresholds) == 0 {\n\t\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Eviction manager: no resources are starved\")\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// rank the thresholds by eviction priority\n\tsort.Sort(byEvictionPriority(thresholds))\n\tthresholdToReclaim, resourceToReclaim, foundAny := getReclaimableThreshold(thresholds)\n\tif !foundAny {\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: attempting to reclaim\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n\n\t// record an event about the resources we are now attempting to reclaim via eviction\n\tm.recorder.Eventf(m.nodeRef, v1.EventTypeWarning, \"EvictionThresholdMet\", \"Attempting to reclaim %s\", resourceToReclaim)\n\n\t// check if there are node-level resources we can reclaim to reduce pressure before evicting end-user pods.\n\tif m.reclaimNodeLevelResources(ctx, thresholdToReclaim.Signal, resourceToReclaim) {\n\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: able to reduce resource pressure without evicting pods.\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: must evict pod(s) to reclaim\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim)\n\n\t// rank the pods for eviction\n\trank, ok := m.signalToRankFunc[thresholdToReclaim.Signal]\n\tif !ok {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \"Eviction manager: no ranking function for signal\", \"threshold\", thresholdToReclaim.Signal)\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// the only candidates viable for eviction are those pods that had anything running.\n\tif len(activePods) == 0 {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \"Eviction manager: eviction thresholds have been met, but no pods are active to evict\")\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// rank the running pods for eviction for the specified resource\n\trank(activePods, statsFunc)\n\n\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: pods ranked for eviction\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(activePods))\n\n\t//record age of metrics for met thresholds that we are using for evictions.\n\tfor _, t := range thresholds {\n\t\ttimeObserved := observations[t.Signal].time\n\t\tif !timeObserved.IsZero() {\n\t\t\tmetrics.EvictionStatsAge.WithLabelValues(string(t.Signal)).Observe(metrics.SinceInSeconds(timeObserved.Time))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// we kill at most a single pod during each eviction interval\n\tfor i := range activePods {\n\t\tpod := activePods[i]\n\t\tgracePeriodOverride := int64(immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds)\n\t\tif !isHardEvictionThreshold(thresholdToReclaim) {\n\t\t\tgracePeriodOverride = m.config.MaxPodGracePeriodSeconds\n\t\t\tif pod.Spec.TerminationGracePeriodSeconds != nil && !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.AllowOverwriteTerminationGracePeriodSeconds) {\n\t\t\t\tgracePeriodOverride = min(m.config.MaxPodGracePeriodSeconds, *pod.Spec.TerminationGracePeriodSeconds)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tmessage, annotations := evictionMessage(resourceToReclaim, pod, statsFunc, thresholds, observations)\n\t\tcondition := &v1.PodCondition{\n\t\t\tType:    v1.DisruptionTarget,\n\t\t\tStatus:  v1.ConditionTrue,\n\t\t\tReason:  v1.PodReasonTerminationByKubelet,\n\t\t\tMessage: message,\n\t\t}\n\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, gracePeriodOverride, message, annotations, condition) {\n\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(string(thresholdToReclaim.Signal)).Inc()\n\t\t\treturn []*v1.Pod{pod}, nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: unable to evict any pods from the node\")\n\treturn nil, nil\n}\n\nfunc (m *managerImpl) waitForPodsCleanup(podCleanedUpFunc PodCleanedUpFunc, pods []*v1.Pod) {\n\ttimeout := m.clock.NewTimer(podCleanupTimeout)\n\tdefer timeout.Stop()\n\tticker := m.clock.NewTicker(podCleanupPollFreq)\n\tdefer ticker.Stop()\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-timeout.C():\n\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: timed out waiting for pods to be cleaned up\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods))\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\tcase <-ticker.C():\n\t\t\tfor i, pod := range pods {\n\t\t\t\tif !podCleanedUpFunc(pod) {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tif i == len(pods)-1 {\n\t\t\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: pods successfully cleaned up\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods))\n\t\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// reclaimNodeLevelResources attempts to reclaim node level resources.  returns true if thresholds were satisfied and no pod eviction is required.\nfunc (m *managerImpl) reclaimNodeLevelResources(ctx context.Context, signalToReclaim evictionapi.Signal, resourceToReclaim v1.ResourceName) bool {\n\tnodeReclaimFuncs := m.signalToNodeReclaimFuncs[signalToReclaim]\n\tfor _, nodeReclaimFunc := range nodeReclaimFuncs {\n\t\t// attempt to reclaim the pressured resource.\n\t\tif err := nodeReclaimFunc(ctx); err != nil {\n\t\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: unexpected error when attempting to reduce resource pressure\", \"resourceName\", resourceToReclaim, \"err\", err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t}\n\tif len(nodeReclaimFuncs) > 0 {\n\t\tsummary, err := m.summaryProvider.Get(ctx, true)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Eviction manager: failed to get summary stats after resource reclaim\")\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n\t\tobservations, _ := makeSignalObservations(summary)\n\t\tdebugLogObservations(\"observations after resource reclaim\", observations)\n\n\t\t// evaluate all thresholds independently of their grace period to see if with\n\t\t// the new observations, we think we have met min reclaim goals\n\t\tthresholds := thresholdsMet(m.config.Thresholds, observations, true)\n\t\tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(\"thresholds after resource reclaim - ignoring grace period\", thresholds, observations)\n\n\t\tif len(thresholds) == 0 {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\n// localStorageEviction checks the EmptyDir volume usage for each pod and determine whether it exceeds the specified limit and needs\n// to be evicted. It also checks every container in the pod, if the container overlay usage exceeds the limit, the pod will be evicted too.\nfunc (m *managerImpl) localStorageEviction(pods []*v1.Pod, statsFunc statsFunc) []*v1.Pod {\n\tevicted := []*v1.Pod{}\n\tfor _, pod := range pods {\n\t\tpodStats, ok := statsFunc(pod)\n\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif m.emptyDirLimitEviction(podStats, pod) {\n\t\t\tevicted = append(evicted, pod)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif m.podEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats, pod) {\n\t\t\tevicted = append(evicted, pod)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif m.containerEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats, pod) {\n\t\t\tevicted = append(evicted, pod)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn evicted\n}\n\nfunc (m *managerImpl) emptyDirLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n\tpodVolumeUsed := make(map[string]*resource.Quantity)\n\tfor _, volume := range podStats.VolumeStats {\n\t\tpodVolumeUsed[volume.Name] = resource.NewQuantity(int64(*volume.UsedBytes), resource.BinarySI)\n\t}\n\tfor i := range pod.Spec.Volumes {\n\t\tsource := &pod.Spec.Volumes[i].VolumeSource\n\t\tif source.EmptyDir != nil {\n\t\t\tsize := source.EmptyDir.SizeLimit\n\t\t\tused := podVolumeUsed[pod.Spec.Volumes[i].Name]\n\t\t\tif used != nil && size != nil && size.Sign() == 1 && used.Cmp(*size) > 0 {\n\t\t\t\t// the emptyDir usage exceeds the size limit, evict the pod\n\t\t\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, fmt.Sprintf(emptyDirMessageFmt, pod.Spec.Volumes[i].Name, size.String()), nil, nil) {\n\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEmptyDirFsLimit).Inc()\n\t\t\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc (m *managerImpl) podEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n\tpodLimits := resourcehelper.PodLimits(pod, resourcehelper.PodResourcesOptions{})\n\t_, found := podLimits[v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage]\n\tif !found {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// pod stats api summarizes ephemeral storage usage (container, emptyDir, host[etc-hosts, logs])\n\tpodEphemeralStorageTotalUsage := &resource.Quantity{}\n\tif podStats.EphemeralStorage != nil && podStats.EphemeralStorage.UsedBytes != nil {\n\t\tpodEphemeralStorageTotalUsage = resource.NewQuantity(int64(*podStats.EphemeralStorage.UsedBytes), resource.BinarySI)\n\t}\n\tpodEphemeralStorageLimit := podLimits[v1.ResourceEphemeralStorage]\n\tif podEphemeralStorageTotalUsage.Cmp(podEphemeralStorageLimit) > 0 {\n\t\t// the total usage of pod exceeds the total size limit of containers, evict the pod\n\t\tmessage := fmt.Sprintf(podEphemeralStorageMessageFmt, podEphemeralStorageLimit.String())\n\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, message, nil, nil) {\n\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEphemeralPodFsLimit).Inc()\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc (m *managerImpl) containerEphemeralStorageLimitEviction(podStats statsapi.PodStats, pod *v1.Pod) bool {\n\tthresholdsMap := make(map[string]*resource.Quantity)\n\tfor _, container := range pod.Spec.Containers {\n\t\tephemeralLimit := container.Resources.Limits.StorageEphemeral()\n\t\tif ephemeralLimit != nil && ephemeralLimit.Value() != 0 {\n\t\t\tthresholdsMap[container.Name] = ephemeralLimit\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, containerStat := range podStats.Containers {\n\t\tcontainerUsed := diskUsage(containerStat.Logs)\n\t\tif !*m.dedicatedImageFs {\n\t\t\tcontainerUsed.Add(*diskUsage(containerStat.Rootfs))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif ephemeralStorageThreshold, ok := thresholdsMap[containerStat.Name]; ok {\n\t\t\tif ephemeralStorageThreshold.Cmp(*containerUsed) < 0 {\n\t\t\t\tif m.evictPod(pod, immediateEvictionGracePeriodSeconds, fmt.Sprintf(containerEphemeralStorageMessageFmt, containerStat.Name, ephemeralStorageThreshold.String()), nil, nil) {\n\t\t\t\t\tmetrics.Evictions.WithLabelValues(signalEphemeralContainerFsLimit).Inc()\n\t\t\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc (m *managerImpl) evictPod(pod *v1.Pod, gracePeriodOverride int64, evictMsg string, annotations map[string]string, condition *v1.PodCondition) bool {\n\t// If the pod is marked as critical and static, and support for critical pod annotations is enabled,\n\t// do not evict such pods. Static pods are not re-admitted after evictions.\n\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/issues/40573 has more details.\n\tif kubelettypes.IsCriticalPod(pod) {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(nil, \"Eviction manager: cannot evict a critical pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\t// record that we are evicting the pod\n\tm.recorder.AnnotatedEventf(pod, annotations, v1.EventTypeWarning, Reason, evictMsg)\n\t// this is a blocking call and should only return when the pod and its containers are killed.\n\tklog.V(3).InfoS(\"Evicting pod\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"podUID\", pod.UID, \"message\", evictMsg)\n\terr := m.killPodFunc(pod, true, &gracePeriodOverride, func(status *v1.PodStatus) {\n\t\tstatus.Phase = v1.PodFailed\n\t\tstatus.Reason = Reason\n\t\tstatus.Message = evictMsg\n\t\tif condition != nil {\n\t\t\tpodutil.UpdatePodCondition(status, condition)\n\t\t}\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(err, \"Eviction manager: pod failed to evict\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\t} else {\n\t\tklog.InfoS(\"Eviction manager: pod is evicted successfully\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod))\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n","numLines":631,"startLine":1,"totalLines":631}}}
